The main attractions in Huai'an: the former residence of the Prime Minister, Huai'an Prefecture Office, Hexia Ancient Town, the No. 1 Scholar's Mansion, and the former residence of Wu Cheng'en are relatively concentrated, all in the southern Huai'an District. After a whole day of walking during the day, in order to take a boat to cruise the inner canal at night and experience the night view of "the canal is three thousand miles long, and the most beautiful is Huai'an", I chose the Jinling Hotel in Huaiyin District at night. This choice is undoubtedly correct. The hotel belongs to the Jinling Group, with a beautiful environment, complete facilities, clean and hygienic, especially considerate service, which reflects the heritage of a five-star hotel everywhere. Special thanks to the front desk staff for arranging a very quiet room. The bed and pillow are very comfortable, allowing me, a person with sleep disorders, to sleep all night. It is really good, and I will choose the Jinling brand in the future.
